        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            document.querySelectorAll('.learn-tabs-wrapper').forEach(wrapper => {
                const panels = wrapper.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel');
                if (!panels.length) return;

                const titlesWrapper = document.createElement('div');
                titlesWrapper.className = 'tabs-titles-wrapper';

                const titlesContainer = document.createElement('div');
                titlesContainer.className = 'tabs-titles';

                titlesWrapper.appendChild(titlesContainer);


                panels.forEach((panel, index) => {
                    const titleEl = panel.querySelector('h1,h2,h3,h4,h5,h6');
                    const titleText = titleEl?.textContent?.trim() || `Tab ${index + 1}`;
                    if (titleEl) titleEl.style.display = 'none'; // sakrij naslov unutar panela

                    const btn = document.createElement('button');
                    btn.className = 'tab-title-button';
                    btn.textContent = titleText;

                    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                        panels.forEach(p => p.style.display = 'none');
                        wrapper.querySelectorAll('.tab-title-button').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
                        panel.style.display = 'block';
                        btn.classList.add('active');
                    });

                    if (index === 0) {
                        btn.classList.add('active');
                        panel.style.display = 'block';
                    } else {
                        panel.style.display = 'none';
                    }

                    titlesContainer.appendChild(btn);
                });

                wrapper.insertBefore(titlesWrapper, wrapper.firstChild);
            });
            function slugify(text) {
                return text.toLowerCase()
                    .trim()
                    .replace(/[^\w\s-]/g, '')
                    .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
                    .replace(/--+/g, '-');
            }

            document.querySelectorAll('h3.check').forEach(function (el) {
                let checkId = el.dataset.checkId;

                if (!checkId) {
                    const slug = slugify(el.innerText);
                    checkId = `exercise-${slug}`;
                    el.dataset.checkId = checkId;
                }

                if (window.exerciseChecked?.includes(checkId)) {
                    el.classList.add('checked');
                }

                el.style.cursor = 'pointer';

                el.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    fetch('/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                        method: 'POST',
                        credentials: 'same-origin',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
                        body: new URLSearchParams({
                            action: 'toggle_exercise_check',
                            check_id: checkId,
                            lesson_id: window.lessonId
                        })
                    })
                        .then(res => res.json())
                        .then(data => {
                            if (data.success) {
                                el.classList.toggle('checked', data.data.checked);
                            }
                        });
                });
            });

            var thumbs = document.querySelectorAll('.custom-video-thumbnail');
            var popup = document.getElementById('videoPopup');
            var container = document.getElementById('videoContainer');
            var closeBtn = document.querySelector('.popup-close');
            var overlay = document.querySelector('.popup-overlay');

            thumbs.forEach(function (thumb) {
                var iframe = thumb.querySelector('iframe');
                if (iframe) iframe.remove();

                thumb.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    var videoId = thumb.getAttribute('data-vid');
                    var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                    var separator = videoId.includes('?') ? '&' : '?';
                    iframe.src = 'https://player.vimeo.com/video/' + videoId + separator + 'autoplay=1';
                    iframe.allow = 'autoplay; fullscreen';
                    iframe.allowFullscreen = true;
                    iframe.frameBorder = 0;

                    container.innerHTML = '';
                    container.appendChild(iframe);
                    popup.style.display = 'flex';
                });
            });

            function closePopup() {
                popup.style.display = 'none';
                container.innerHTML = '';
            }

            closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closePopup);
            overlay.addEventListener('click', closePopup);
        });

    
    jQuery(function($){
                    });
</script>

<script>
    window.onload = function() {
            };
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        const links = document.querySelectorAll('a[href]');

        links.forEach(function (link) {
            if (link.classList.contains('no-blank')) {
                return;
            }

            const url = new URL(link.href, window.location.href);

            if (url.hostname !== window.location.hostname) {
                link.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
                link.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener');
            } else {
                link.removeAttribute('target');
            }
        });
    });
</script>
